 is
 desh kii satta banane or bigaadane kii takat aresas rakhata he, yahi vajah he ki bijepi ke diggaj netaa or modi sarkaar ke mantri bhi sangh ke aage natmastak najar aate hai

 is maukey par ye samajhnaa jaruri he ki aakhir sangh kii sthapana kaise or kab hui or kis tarah ye sanghathan aap 9 dashakon baad duniya ke sabase bade sanghathan ke rup main khud ko sthapit kar chukaa he
 Rashtriya Swayamsevak Sangh, the world's largest voluntary organization, was founded by Keshav Balaram Hedgewar
 bharat ko hindu raashtra banane ke lakshya ke saath 27 sitambar 1925 ko vijaydashami ke din aresas kii sthapana kii gai thi
 This year, on the day of Vijayadashami, the Sangh has completed 93 years of its establishment and in 2025 this organization will become 100 years old
 nagpur ke akhaadon se taiyaar hua sangh maujuuda samay main viraat rup le chukaa he
 Started by less than three dozen people, Hedgewar, the first Sarsanghchalak of the Sangh, planned to form the Sangh in a seminar with 17 people at his home
 is baithak main headgavar ke saath vishwanath kelkar, bhauji kaaware, anna saahane, balaji huddaar, baapuro bhedi aadi maujuud the
 What would be the name of the Sangh, what would be the activities? Everything was gradually fixed over time
 us vakt hinduon ko sirf sangathit karne kaa vichaar tha
 Even the RSS was christened 'rashtriya Swayamsevak Sangh' on 17 April 1926
 isi din headgavar ko sarvasammati se sangh pramukh chunaa gaya, lekin vah sarasanghachaalak november 1929 main banaae gaye
 Such was the name RSS National self-service Association, this name was brainstormed before coming into existence
 rashtriya swayamsevak sangh, jaripatka mandalaur bharatoddharak mandal in teen naamon par vichaar hua
 Out of the 26 members present at the meeting, the RSS came into existence after the voting took place
 'namaste sadaa vatsale mathrubhume' prarthana ke saath pichley kai dashakon se lagaataar desh ke kone-kone main sangh kii shakhayein lag rahi hai
 Hedgewar carried on the union work through gymnasiums or akharas
 swasth or sugathit swayamsevak hona unki kalpana main tha
 The RSS claims the RSS has more than 10 million trained members
 sangh parivaar main 80 se zyada samavichaari yaa anushangik sanghathan hai
 The association is active in about 40 countries of the world
 maujuuda samay main sangh kii 56 hajaar 569 dainik shakhaaen lagati hai
 There are also about 13 thousand 847 weekly congregations and 9 thousand monthly branches
 sangh main sadasyon kaa panjikaran nahin hota
 Based on the presence of such branches, it is estimated that currently more than 50 lakh volunteers regularly visit the branches
 desh kii har tehsil or kareeb 55 hajaar gaanvon main shakha lag rahi he
 Ban on Sangh thrice Sangh made many achievements in its long journey, while it was banned three times
 rashtrapita mahatma gandhi kii hatya ko sangh se jodakar dekha gaya, sangh ke duusare sarasanghachaalak guru golwalkar ko bandi banaaya gaya
 But the ban was lifted from the union after 18 months
 duusari baar apatkaal ke dauraan 1975 se 1977 tak sangh par pabandi lagi

 sangh ne shuru se alag rasta akhriyaar kiyaarees naa to gandhi kii aguwai main chalane vaale andolan main hissedaar bana, na congress se nikle netaji subhash chandra bose ke andolan main saajhedaar

 On 22 July 1947, when the tricolor was considered the national flag, it was fiercely opposed by The Organization
 kaaphi lambey samay tak sangh tirangaa nahin fahraata tha

 yahaan tak ki aresas ne apane dhur virodhiyon ko bhi apane manch par jagah dena shuru kiya he
 It was also a face of the Sangh, which gradually established its identity as a disciplined and nationalist organization
 1962 main china ke dhokhe se kiye hamale se desh sann rah gaya tha
 At that time, the RSS had helped deliver logistics to the border areas
 isse prabhavit hokar pradhanmantri nehru ne 1963 main ganatantr diwas kii parade main sangh ko bulaayaa tha

 1977 main aresas ne purv pradhanmantri indira gandhi ko vivekanand rock memorial kaa udghaatan karne ke liye bulaayaa tha
 The RSS clearly speaks of strengthening Hindu society based on its religion and culture
 sangh se nikle swayamsevakon ne hi bijepi ko sthapit kiya

 desh bhar main path sanchalan nikalate hai
